So he schemed to obtain him for his own land, sending to him a man from among those who had apostatized and were with him. When he reached him, he showed him that his intentions toward Islam and its people had become good, until he had gained his trust. Then one day the two of them went out walking along the seashore, the man having arranged with another agent of the King of Rome to help him seize him. When the two of them closed in on him to take him, he raised his gaze to the sky and said: O Allah, this man has deceived me only by invoking You, so protect me from the two of them by whatever means You will. He said: Then two lions came out toward them and seized them both, and the man returned safely.

As for His saying, Most High: {and makes you successors upon the earth}, that is: He causes one generation to succeed another generation before it, and a later people to succeed an earlier people, as the Almighty said: {If He willed, He could do away with you and produce after you whatever He wills, just as He produced you from the descendants of another people} [al-An'am: 133], and He said: {And it is He who has made you successors upon the earth and raised some of you above others in degrees} [al-An'am: 165], and He said: {And when your Lord said to the angels, indeed I am going to place upon the earth a khalifa (successor)} [al-Baqara: 30], meaning: a people, one succeeding another, as we established previously. Likewise this verse: {and makes you successors upon the earth}, meaning: nation after nation, generation after generation, people after people. Had He willed, He could have brought them all into existence at one time, without making some of them descendants of others; rather, had He willed, He could have created them all together at once, just as He created Adam from dust. And had He willed to make some of them descendants of others, He could have caused none of them to die until the death of all of them came at one and the same time, but then the earth would have grown too narrow for them, and their livelihoods and means of earning would have grown too narrow, and they would have harmed one another. But His wisdom and power decreed that He should create them from a single soul, then multiply them to the utmost degree, scatter them across the earth, and make them generations after generations, and nations after nations, until the appointed term is completed and creation is exhausted, just as the Blessed and Almighty has decreed, and just as He has counted them and numbered them precisely. Then He will establish the Hour, and He will pay every doer in full for his deeds when the decree reaches its appointed term. Therefore the Almighty said: {Or is it He who answers the distressed one when he calls upon Him and removes evil and makes you successors upon the earth? Is there a god besides Allah}, that is: who is able to do that, or is there a god besides Allah who is worshipped, when it is known that Allah alone is the one who does that uniquely. {Little do you remember}, that is: how little is their remembrance regarding what would guide them to the truth and lead them to the straight path.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُنَبِّهُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ هُوَ المدعُوّ عِنْدَ الشَّدَائِدِ، المرجُوّ عِنْدَ النَّوَازِلِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا مَسَّكُمُ الضُّرُّ فِي الْبَحْرِ ضَلَّ مَنْ تَدْعُونَ إِلا إِيَّاهُ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٦٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ إِذَا مَسَّكُمُ الضُّرُّ فَإِلَيْهِ تَجْأَرُونَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٥٣] . وَهَكَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿أَمَّنْ يُجِيبُ الْمُضْطَرَّ إِذَا دَعَاهُ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ هُوَ الَّذِي لَا يَلْجَأُ الْمُضْطَرُّ إِلَّا إِلَيْهِ، وَالَّذِي لَا يَكْشِفُ ضُرَّ الْمَضْرُورِينَ سِوَاهُ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا وُهَيْب، حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدٌ الحَذّاء، عَنْ أَبِي تَمِيمَةَ الهُجَيْمي، عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ بَلْهُجَيْمٍ قَالَ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِلَامَ تَدْعُو؟ قَالَ: "أَدْعُو إِلَى اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ، الَّذِي إِنْ مَسّك ضُرٌّ فَدَعَوْتَهُ كَشَفَ عَنْكَ، وَالَّذِي إِنْ أضْلَلْت بِأَرْضٍ قَفْر فدعوتَه رَدّ عَلَيْكَ، وَالَّذِي إِنْ أَصَابَتْكَ سَنة فدعوتَه أنبتَ لَكَ". قَالَ: قُلْتُ: أَوْصِنِي. قَالَ: "لَا تَسُبَّنَّ أَحَدًا، وَلَا تَزْهَدنّ فِي الْمَعْرُوفِ، وَلَوْ أَنْ تَلْقَى أَخَاكَ وَأَنْتَ مُنْبَسِطٌ إِلَيْهِ وَجْهَكَ، وَلَوْ أَنْ تُفرغَ مِنْ دَلوك فِي إِنَاءِ المستقي، وَاتَّزِرْ إِلَى نِصْفِ السَّاقِ، فَإِنْ أَبَيْتَ فَإِلَى الْكَعْبَيْنِ. وَإِيَّاكَ وَإِسْبَالَ الْإِزَارِ، فَإِنَّ إِسْبَالَ الْإِزَارِ مِنَ الْمَخِيلَةِ، [وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ -تَبَارَكَ تَعَالَى -لَا يُحِبُّ الْمَخِيلَةَ] .

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، فَذَكَرَ اسْمَ الصَّحَابِيِّ فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ -هُوَ ابْنُ عُبَيْدٍ -حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدَةُ الهُجَيْمي عَنْ أَبِي تَميمَةَ الهُجَيْمي، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ سُلَيم الهُجَيمي قَالَ: أَتَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ مُحْتَبٍ بِشَمْلَة، وَقَدْ وَقَعَ هُدْبها عَلَى قَدَمَيْهِ، فَقُلْتُ: أَيُّكُمْ مُحَمَّدٌ -أَوْ: رَسُولُ اللَّهِ؟ -فَأَوْمَأَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى نَفْسِهِ، فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَنَا مِنْ أَهْلِ الْبَادِيَةِ، وفِيَّ جَفَاؤُهُمْ، فَأَوْصِنِي. فَقَالَ: "لَا تحقرَنّ مِنَ الْمَعْرُوفِ شَيْئًا، وَلَوْ أَنْ تَلْقَى أَخَاكَ وَوَجْهُكَ مُنْبَسط، وَلَوْ أَنْ تُفْرِغَ مِنْ دَلْوِكَ فِي إِنَاءِ الْمُسْتَقِي، وَإِنِ امْرُؤٌ شَتَمك بِمَا يَعْلَمُ فِيكَ فَلَا تَشْتِمْهُ بِمَا تَعْلَمُ فِيهِ، فَإِنَّهُ يَكُونُ لَكَ أَجْرُهُ وَعَلَيْهِ وزْرُه. وَإِيَّاكَ وَإِسْبَالَ الْإِزَارِ، فَإِنَّ إِسْبَالَ الْإِزَارِ مِنَ المَخيلَة، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمَخِيلَةَ، وَلَا تَسُبَّنّ أَحَدًا". قَالَ: فَمَا سَبَبْتُ بَعْدَهُ أَحَدًا، وَلَا شَاةً وَلَا بَعِيرًا .

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ لِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ طُرُقًا، وَعِنْدَهُمَا طَرَفٌ صَالِحٌ مِنْهُ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ هَاشِمٍ حَدَّثَنَا عبدَةَ بْنُ نُوحٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْحَجَّاجِ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي صَالِحٍ قَالَ: دَخَلَ عليَّ طَاوُسٌ يَعُودُنِي، فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: ادْعُ اللَّهَ لِي يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ. فَقَالَ: ادْعُ لِنَفْسِكَ، فَإِنَّهُ يُجِيبُ الْمُضْطَرَّ إِذَا دَعَاهُ.

وَقَالَ وَهْبُ بْنُ مُنَبِّهٍ: قَرَأْتُ فِي الْكِتَابِ الْأَوَّلِ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: بِعِزَّتِي إِنَّهُ مَنِ اعْتَصَمَ بِي فَإِنْ كَادَتْهُ السَّمَوَاتُ وَمَنْ فِيهِنَّ، وَالْأَرْضُ بِمَنْ فِيهَا، فَإِنِّي أَجْعَلُ لَهُ مِنْ بَيْنِ ذَلِكَ مَخْرَجًا. وَمَنْ لَمْ يَعْتَصِمْ بِي فَإِنِّي أَخْسِفُ بِهِ مِنْ تَحْتِ قَدَمَيْهِ الْأَرْضَ، فَأَجْعَلُهُ فِي الْهَوَاءِ، فَأَكِلُهُ إِلَى نَفْسِهِ.

وَذَكَرَ الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ رَجُلٍ -حَكَى عَنْهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ الدّينَوَري، الْمَعْرُوفُ بالدّقّيِّ الصُّوفِيُّ -قَالَ هَذَا الرَّجُلُ : كُنْتُ أُكَارِي عَلَى بَغْلٍ لِي مِنْ دِمَشْقَ إِلَى بَلَدِ الزّبَدَاني، فَرَكِبَ مَعِي ذَاتَ مَرَّةٍ رَجُلٌ، فَمَرَرْنَا عَلَى بَعْضِ الطَّرِيقِ، عَلَى طَرِيقٍ غَيْرِ مَسْلُوكَةٍ، فَقَالَ لِي: خُذْ فِي هَذِهِ، فَإِنَّهَا أَقْرَبُ. فَقُلْتُ: لَا خبرَةَ لِي فِيهَا، فَقَالَ: بَلْ هِيَ أَقْرَبُ. فَسَلَكْنَاهَا فَانْتَهَيْنَا إِلَى مَكَانٍ وَعْر وَوَادٍ عَمِيقٍ، وَفِيهِ قَتْلَى كَثِيرٌ، فَقَالَ لِي: أَمْسِكْ رَأْسَ الْبَغْلِ حَتَّى أَنْزِلَ. فَنَزَلَ وَتَشَمَّرَ، وَجَمَعَ عَلَيْهِ ثِيَابَهُ، وَسَلَّ سِكِّينًا مَعَهُ وَقَصَدَنِي، فَفَرَرْتُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَتَبِعَنِي، فَنَاشَدْتُهُ اللَّهَ وَقُلْتُ: خُذِ الْبَغْلَ بِمَا عَلَيْهِ. فَقَالَ: هُوَ لِي، وَإِنَّمَا أُرِيدُ قَتْلَكَ. فَخَوَّفْتُهُ اللَّهَ وَالْعُقُوبَةَ فَلَمْ يَقْبَلْ، فَاسْتَسْلَمْتُ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ وَقُلْتُ: إِنْ رَأَيْتَ أَنْ تَتْرُكَنِي حَتَّى أُصَلِّيَ رَكْعَتَيْنِ؟ فَقَالَ: [صَلِّ] وَعَجِّلْ. فقمت أصلي فَأرْتِج عليَّ الْقُرْآنُ فَلَمْ يَحضرني مِنْهُ حَرْفٌ وَاحِدٌ، فَبَقِيتُ وَاقِفًا مُتَحَيِّرًا وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: هِيهِ. افرُغ. فَأَجْرَى اللَّهُ عَلَى لِسَانِي قَوْلَهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَمَّنْ يُجِيبُ الْمُضْطَرَّ إِذَا دَعَاهُ وَيَكْشِفُ السُّوءَ﴾ ، فَإِذَا أَنَا بِفَارِسٍ قَدْ أَقْبَلَ مِنْ فَمِ الْوَادِي، وَبِيَدِهِ حَرْبَةٌ، فَرَمَى بِهَا الرَّجُلَ فَمَا أَخْطَأَتْ فُؤَادَهُ، فَخَرَّ صَرِيعًا، فَتَعَلَّقْتُ بِالْفَارِسِ وَقُلْتُ: بِاللَّهِ مَنْ أَنْتَ؟ فَقَالَ: أَنَا رَسُولُ [اللَّهِ] الَّذِي يُجِيبُ الْمُضْطَرَّ إِذَا دَعَاهُ، وَيَكْشِفُ السُّوءَ. قَالَ: فَأَخَذْتُ الْبَغْلَ وَالْحَمْلَ وَرَجَعْتُ سَالِمًا.

وَذُكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "فَاطِمَةَ بِنْتِ الْحَسَنِ أَمِّ أَحْمَدَ الْعِجْلِيَّةِ" قَالَتْ: هَزَمَ الْكَفَّارُ يَوْمًا الْمُسْلِمِينَ فِي غَزَاةٍ، فَوَقَفَ جَوَاد جَيّد بِصَاحِبِهِ، وَكَانَ مِنْ ذَوِي الْيَسَارِ وَمِنَ الصُّلَحَاءِ، فَقَالَ لِلْجَوَادِ: مَا لَكَ؟ وَيْلَكَ. إِنَّمَا كُنْتُ أَعُدُّكَ لِمِثْلِ هَذَا الْيَوْمِ. فَقَالَ لَهُ الْجَوَادُ: وَمَا لِيَ لَا أُقَصِّرُ وَأَنْتَ تَكلُ عَلُوفَتِي إِلَى السُّوَّاسِ فَيَظْلِمُونَنِي وَلَا يُطْعِمُونَنِي إِلَّا الْقَلِيلَ؟ فَقَالَ: لَكَ عليَّ عَهْدُ اللَّهِ أَنِّي لَا أَعْلُفُكَ بَعْدَ هَذَا الْيَوْمِ إِلَّا فِي حِجْري. فَجَرَى الْجَوَادُ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ، ونجَّى صَاحِبَهُ، وَكَانَ لَا يَعْلِفُهُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ إِلَّا فِي حِجْره، وَاشْتَهَرَ أَمْرُهُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ، وَجَعَلُوا يَقْصِدُونَهُ لِيَسْمَعُوا مِنْهُ ذَلِكَ، وَبَلَغَ مَلِكَ الرُّومِ أمرُه، فَقَالَ: مَا تُضَام بَلْدَةٌ يَكُونُ هَذَا الرَّجُلُ فِيهَا. وَاحْتَالَ لِيُحَصِّلَهُ فِي بَلَدِهِ، فَبَعَثَ إِلَيْهِ رَجُلًا مِنَ الْمُرْتَدِّينَ عِنْدَهُ، فَلَمَّا انْتَهَى إِلَيْهِ أَظْهَرَ لَهُ أَنَّهُ قَدْ حَسُنت نِيَّتُهُ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ وَقَوْمِهِ، حَتَّى اسْتَوْثَقَ، ثُمَّ خَرَجَا يَوْمًا يَمْشِيَانِ عَلَى جَنْبِ السَّاحِلِ، وَقَدْ وَاعَدَ شَخْصًا آخَرَ مِنْ جِهَةِ مَلِكِ الرُّومِ لِيَتَسَاعَدَا عَلَى أَسْرِهِ، فَلَمَّا اكْتَنَفَاهُ لِيَأْخُذَاهُ رَفَع طَرْفَهُ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ وَقَالَ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنَّهُ إِنَّمَا خَدَعني بِكَ فَاكْفِنِيهِمَا بِمَا شِئْتَ، قَالَ: فَخَرَجَ سَبُعَانِ إِلَيْهِمَا فَأَخَذَاهُمَا، وَرَجَعَ الرَّجُلُ سَالِمًا .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَجْعَلُكُمْ خُلَفَاءَ الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: يُخْلفُ قَرنا لِقَرْنٍ قَبْلَهُمْ وخَلَفًا لِسَلَفٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ وَيَسْتَخْلِفْ مِنْ بَعْدِكُمْ مَا يَشَاءُ كَمَا أَنْشَأَكُمْ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ قَوْمٍ آخَرِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٣٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي جَعَلَكُمْ خَلائِفَ الأرْضِ وَرَفَعَ بَعْضَكُمْ فَوْقَ بَعْضٍ دَرَجَاتٍ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٦٥] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلائِكَةِ إِنِّي جَاعِلٌ فِي الأرْضِ خَلِيفَةً﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٣٠] ، أَيْ: قَوْمًا يَخْلُفُ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا كَمَا قَدَّمْنَا تَقْرِيرَهُ. وَهَكَذَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَيَجْعَلُكُمْ خُلَفَاءَ الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: أُمَّةً بَعْدَ أُمَّةٍ، وَجِيلًا بَعْدَ جِيلٍ، وَقَوْمًا بَعْدَ قَوْمٍ. وَلَوْ شَاءَ لَأَوْجَدَهُمْ كُلَّهُمْ فِي وَقْتٍ وَاحِدٍ، وَلَمْ يَجْعَلْ بعضَهم مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ بَعْضٍ، بَلْ لَوْ شَاءَ لَخَلَقَهُمْ كُلَّهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، كَمَا خَلَقَ آدَمَ مِنْ تُرَابٍ. وَلَوْ شَاءَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَهُمْ بَعْضَهُمْ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ بَعْضٍ وَلَكِنْ لَا يُمِيتُ أَحَدًا حَتَّى تَكُونَ وَفَاةُ الْجَمِيعِ فِي وَقْتٍ وَاحِدٍ، فَكَانَتْ تَضِيقُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْأَرْضُ وَتَضِيقُ عَلَيْهِمْ مَعَايِشُهُمْ وَأَكْسَابُهُمْ، وَيَتَضَرَّرُ بَعْضُهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ. وَلَكِنِ اقْتَضَتْ حِكْمَتُهُ وَقُدْرَتُهُ أَنْ يَخْلُقَهُمْ مِنْ نَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ، ثُمَّ يُكْثِرَهُمْ غَايَةَ الْكَثْرَةِ، وَيَذْرَأَهُمْ فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَيَجْعَلَهُمْ قُرُونًا بَعْدَ قُرُونٍ، وَأُمَمًا بَعْدَ أُمَمٍ، حَتَّى يَنْقَضِيَ الْأَجَلُ وَتَفْرُغَ البَرية، كَمَا قَدَّرَ ذَلِكَ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، وَكَمَا أَحْصَاهُمْ وعَدّهم عَدًا، ثُمَّ يُقِيمُ الْقِيَامَةَ، ويُوفي كُلَّ عَامِلٍ عمله إذا بلغ الكتاب أَجَلَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَمَّنْ يُجِيبُ الْمُضْطَرَّ إِذَا دَعَاهُ وَيَكْشِفُ السُّوءَ وَيَجْعَلُكُمْ خُلَفَاءَ الأرْضِ أَإِلَهٌ مَعَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: يَقْدِرُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، أَوْ إِلَهٌ مَعَ اللَّهِ يُعْبد، وَقَدْ عُلِمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْمُتَفَرِّدُ بِفِعْلِ ذَلِكَ ﴿قَلِيلا مَا تَذَكَّرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا أَقَلَّ تَذَكُّرَهُمْ فِيمَا يُرْشِدُهُمْ إِلَى الْحَقِّ، وَيَهْدِيهِمْ إِلَى الصِّرَاطِ الْمُسْتَقِيمِ.

---

## 27:63 — verse 63

### Translation

He says: {Or, Who guides you in the darknesses of land and sea} that is, by what He has created of heavenly and earthly signs, as He said: {and landmarks, and by the stars they are guided} [al-Nahl: 16], and He, Exalted, said: {And He it is Who has made for you the stars that you may be guided by them in the darknesses of land and sea} the verse [al-An'am: 97].

{And Who sends the winds as glad tidings before His mercy} that is, before the clouds that carry rain, by which He relieves His servants who are afflicted with drought, distress, and despair. {Is there a god together with Allah? Exalted is Allah above what they associate with Him.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ: ﴿أَمَّنْ يَهْدِيكُمْ فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ﴾ أَيْ: بِمَا خَلَقَ مِنَ الدَّلَائِلِ السَّمَاوِيَّةِ وَالْأَرْضِيَّةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَعَلامَاتٍ وَبِالنَّجْمِ هُمْ يَهْتَدُونَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ١٦] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمُ النُّجُومَ لِتَهْتَدُوا بِهَا فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٩٧] .

﴿وَمَنْ يُرْسِلُ الرِّيَاحَ بُشْرًا بَيْنَ يَدَيْ رَحْمَتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بَيْنَ يَدَيِ السَّحَابِ الَّذِي فِيهِ مَطَرٌ، يُغِيثُ بِهِ عِبَادَهُ الْمُجْدِبِينَ الْأَزِلِينَ الْقَنِطِينَ، ﴿أَإِلَهٌ مَعَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى اللَّهُ عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ .

---

## 27:64 — verse 64

### Translation

That is: He is the One who by His power and dominion begins creation and then repeats it, as He said, exalted is He, in another verse: {Indeed, the seizing of your Lord is severe. Indeed, it is He who begins and repeats} [al-Buruj: 12, 13], and He said: {And He is the One who begins creation, then repeats it, and that is easier for Him} [al-Rum: 27].

{And who provides for you from the heaven and the earth}, that is, by what He sends down from the rain of the sky and by what He causes to grow from the blessings of the earth, as He said: {By the sky which returns, and the earth which splits} [al-Tariq: 11, 12], and He said: {He knows what enters into the earth and what comes out of it, and what descends from the sky and what ascends therein} [al-Hadid: 4]. So He, blessed and exalted is He, sends down from the sky blessed water, then settles it in the earth, then brings forth by it various kinds of crops, fruits, flowers, and other varieties of many colors, {Eat and pasture your cattle; indeed in that are signs for people of understanding} [Taha: 54]. Therefore He said: {Is there a god besides Allah} who does this? And according to the other reading: who is worshipped? {Say, bring forth your proof} of the validity of what you claim regarding the worship of other gods, {if you are truthful} in that. And it is already known that they have no argument and no proof, as Allah said: {And whoever calls upon another god besides Allah, having no proof for it, then his reckoning is only with his Lord. Indeed, the disbelievers will not succeed} [al-Mu'minun: 117].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَيْ: هُوَ الَّذِي بِقُدْرَتِهِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ يَبْدَأُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿إِنَّ بَطْشَ رَبِّكَ لَشَدِيدٌ إِنَّهُ هُوَ يُبْدِئُ وَيُعِيدُ﴾ [الْبُرُوجِ: ١٢، ١٣] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَبْدَأُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ وَهُوَ أَهْوَنُ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٢٧] .

﴿وَمَنْ يَرْزُقُكُمْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: بِمَا يُنْزِلُ مِنْ مَطَرِ السَّمَاءِ، وَيُنْبِتُ مِنْ بَرَكَاتِ الْأَرْضِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالسَّمَاءِ ذَاتِ الرَّجْعِ. وَالأرْضِ ذَاتِ الصَّدْعِ﴾ [الطَّارِقِ: ١١، ١٢] ، وَقَالَ ﴿يَعْلَمُ مَا يَلِجُ فِي الأرْضِ وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا وَمَا يَنزلُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَمَا يَعْرُجُ فِيهَا﴾ [الْحَدِيدِ: ٤] ، فَهُوَ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، يُنَزِّلُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً مُبَارَكًا فَيُسْكِنُهُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، ثُمَّ يُخْرِجُ بِهِ [مِنْهَا] أَنْوَاعَ الزُّرُوعِ وَالثِّمَارِ وَالْأَزَاهِيرِ، وَغَيْرَ ذَلِكَ مِنْ أَلْوَانٍ شَتَّى، ﴿كُلُوا وَارْعَوْا أَنْعَامَكُمْ إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لأولِي النُّهَى﴾ [طَهَ: ٥٤] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَإِلَهٌ مَعَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فَعَلَ هَذَا. وَعَلَى الْقَوْلِ الْآخَرِ: يُعْبَدُ؟ ﴿قُلْ هَاتُوا بُرْهَانَكُمْ﴾ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا تَدَّعُونَهُ مِنْ عِبَادَةِ آلِهَةٍ أُخْرَى، ﴿إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَقَدْ عَلِمَ أَنَّهُ لَا حُجَّةَ لَهُمْ وَلَا بُرْهَانَ، كَمَا قَالَ [اللَّهُ] : ﴿وَمَنْ يَدْعُ مَعَ اللَّهِ إِلَهًا آخَرَ لَا بُرْهَانَ لَهُ بِهِ فَإِنَّمَا حِسَابُهُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِ إِنَّهُ لا يُفْلِحُ الْكَافِرُونَ﴾ [المؤمنون: ١١٧] .

---

## 27:65-66 — verses 65-66 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, commanding His Messenger ﷺ to say, teaching all of creation, that no one among the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth knows the unseen. His saying, {except Allah}, is an exception of disjunction (istithna munqati'), meaning: no one knows that except Allah, Mighty and Majestic, for He alone possesses that exclusively, having no partner in it, just as He said: {And with Him are the keys of the unseen; none knows them except Him} [al-An'am: 59], and He said: {Indeed, Allah, with Him is the knowledge of the Hour, and He sends down the rain, and He knows what is in the wombs. And no soul knows what it will earn tomorrow, and no soul knows in what land it will die. Indeed, Allah is Knowing and Aware} [Luqman: 34]. The verses on this subject are numerous.

As for His saying, {And they do not perceive when they will be resurrected}, it means: the creatures dwelling in the heavens and the earth do not perceive the time of the Hour, just as He said: {It weighs heavily upon the heavens and the earth; it will not come upon you except suddenly} [al-A'raf: 187], meaning: knowledge of it weighs heavily upon the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... from A'isha, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: whoever claims that he, meaning the Prophet ﷺ, knows what will happen tomorrow has committed a great lie against Allah, for Allah, the Exalted, says: {None in the heavens and the earth knows the unseen except Allah}.

Qatada said: Allah made these stars for three purposes: He made them an adornment for the sky, He made them a means of guidance, and He made them missiles against the devils. Whoever attributes to them anything beyond that has spoken according to his own opinion, has erred in his portion, has squandered his share, and has undertaken something of which he has no knowledge. There are people ignorant of the command of Allah who have invented from these stars a form of soothsaying: whoever marries under such and such a star, such and such will happen to him; whoever travels under such and such a star, such and such will happen to him; whoever is born under such and such a star, such and such will happen to him. By my life, there is no star under which both the red-skinned and the black-skinned are not born, and the short and the tall, and the handsome and the ugly, and the knowledge of this star, this animal, or this bird has nothing to do with the unseen at all! Allah has decreed that none in the heavens and the earth knows the unseen except Allah, and that they do not perceive when they will be resurrected.

Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this from him word for word, and it is a magnificent, solid, and sound statement.

As for His saying, {Nay, their knowledge of the Hereafter has reached its limit; nay, they are in doubt about it}, it means: their knowledge has come to its end and fallen short of knowing its time.

Others read it as "bal adraka 'ilmuhum" (nay, their knowledge has attained), meaning their knowledge became equal in that regard, as in the sound hadith recorded by Muslim: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to Gabriel (peace be upon him), when he had asked him about the time of the Hour, "The one asked about it is no more knowledgeable than the one asking," meaning: the knowledge of the one asked and the one asking were equal in their inability to grasp that.

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding {Nay, their knowledge of the Hereafter has reached its limit}: meaning, it has vanished.

Qatada said, regarding {Nay, their knowledge of the Hereafter has reached its limit}: meaning, their Lord declares them ignorant; He says that no knowledge of the Hereafter has reached them. This is one interpretation.

Ibn Jurayj said, on the authority of Ata al-Khurasani, from Ibn Abbas, regarding "bal adraka 'ilmuhum fi al-akhirah": when knowledge no longer benefits them. Ata al-Khurasani and al-Suddi said likewise: that their knowledge is only attained and made complete on the Day of Resurrection, where it does them no good, just as the Almighty said: {How well they will hear and how well they will see on the Day they come to Us! But the wrongdoers today are in manifest error} [Maryam: 38].

Sufyan said, from Amr ibn Ubayd, from al-Hasan, that he used to recite it "bal adraka 'ilmuhum" (nay, their knowledge has attained), saying: their knowledge in this world vanished when they beheld the Hereafter with their own eyes.

As for His saying, {Nay, they are in doubt about it}, this refers to the category, meaning the disbelievers, just as the Almighty said: {And they will be presented before your Lord in rows: "You have certainly come to Us just as We created you the first time. Nay, you claimed that We would never make for you an appointed time"} [al-Kahf: 48], meaning the disbelievers among you. Likewise here He says, {Nay, they are in doubt about it}, meaning they doubt its existence and its coming to pass, {Nay, they are blind to it}, meaning they are in great blindness and ignorance regarding its matter and its nature.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا رَسُولَهُ ﷺ أَنْ يَقُولَ مُعَلِّمًا لِجَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ: أَنَّهُ لَا يَعْلَمُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ الْغَيْبَ. وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا اللَّهَ﴾ اسْتِثْنَاءٌ مُنْقَطِعٌ، أَيْ: لَا يَعْلَمُ أَحَدٌ ذَلِكَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَإِنَّهُ الْمُنْفَرِدُ بِذَلِكَ وَحْدَهُ، لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَعِنْدَهُ مَفَاتِحُ الْغَيْبِ لَا يَعْلَمُهَا إِلا هُوَ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٥٩] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ عِنْدَهُ عِلْمُ السَّاعَةِ وَيُنزلُ الْغَيْثَ وَيَعْلَمُ مَا فِي الأرْحَامِ وَمَا تَدْرِي نَفْسٌ مَاذَا تَكْسِبُ غَدًا وَمَا تَدْرِي نَفْسٌ بِأَيِّ أَرْضٍ تَمُوتُ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلِيمٌ خَبِيرٌ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٣٤] ، وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ أَيَّانَ يُبْعَثُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا يَشْعُرُ الْخَلَائِقُ السَّاكِنُونَ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ بِوَقْتِ السَّاعَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿ثَقُلَتْ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ لَا تَأْتِيكُمْ إِلا بَغْتَةً﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٨٧] ، أَيْ: ثَقُلَ عِلْمُهَا عَلَى أَهْلِ السَّمَوَاتُ وَالْأَرْضُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الجَعْد، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عن مسروق، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: مَنْ زَعَمَ أَنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ -يَعْنِي النَّبِيَّ ﷺ -مَا يَكُونُ فِي غَدٍ فَقَدْ أَعْظَمَ عَلَى اللَّهِ الفِرْية؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿لَا يَعْلَمُ مَنْ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ الْغَيْبَ إِلا اللَّهُ﴾ .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: إِنَّمَا جَعَلَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ النُّجُومَ لِثَلَاثِ خَصَلَاتٍ : جَعَلَهَا زِينَةً لِلسَّمَاءِ، وَجَعَلَهَا يُهْتَدَى بِهَا، وَجَعَلَهَا رُجُومًا [لِلشَّيَاطِينِ] ، فَمَنْ تَعَاطَى فِيهَا غَيْرَ ذَلِكَ فَقَدْ قَالَ بِرَأْيِهِ، وَأَخْطَأَ حَظَّهُ، وَأَضَاعَ نَصِيبَهُ وتكلَّف مَا لَا عِلْمَ لَهُ بِهِ. وَإِنَّ نَاسًا جَهَلَة بِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ، قَدْ أَحْدَثُوا مِنْ هَذِهِ النُّجُومِ كِهَانَةً: مَنْ أعْرَس بِنَجْمِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، كَانَ كَذَا وَكَذَا. ومَنْ سَافَرَ بِنَجْمِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، كَانَ كَذَا وَكَذَا. ومَنْ وُلِدَ بِنَجْمِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، كَانَ كَذَا وَكَذَا. وَلَعَمْرِي مَا مِنْ نَجْمٍ إِلَّا يُولَدُ بِهِ الْأَحْمَرُ وَالْأَسْوَدُ، وَالْقَصِيرُ وَالطَّوِيلُ، وَالْحَسَنُ وَالدَّمِيمُ، وَمَا علْمُ هَذَا النَّجْمِ وَهَذِهِ الدَّابَّةِ وَهَذَا الطَّيْرِ بِشَيْءٍ مِنَ الْغَيْبِ! وَقَضَى اللَّهُ: أَنَّهُ لَا يَعْلَمُ مَنْ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ الْغَيْبَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ أَيَّانَ يُبْعَثُونَ.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ عَنْهُ بِحُرُوفِهِ، وَهُوَ كَلَامٌ جَلِيلٌ مَتِينٌ صَحِيحٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلِ ادَّارَكَ عِلْمُهُمْ فِي الآخِرَةِ بَلْ هُمْ فِي شَكٍّ مِنْهَا﴾ أَيِ: انْتَهَى عِلْمُهُمْ وَعَجَزَ عَنْ مَعْرِفَةِ وَقْتِهَا.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: "بَلْ أَدْرَكَ عِلْمُهُمْ"، أَيْ: تَسَاوَى عِلْمُهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ، كَمَا فِي الصَّحِيحِ لِمُسْلِمٍ: أَنَّ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم قال لِجِبْرِيلَ -وَقَدْ سَأَلَهُ عَنْ وَقْتِ السَّاعَةِ -مَا الْمَسْؤُولُ عَنْهَا بِأَعْلَمَ مِنَ السَّائِلِ أَيْ: تَسَاوَى فِي الْعَجْزِ عَنْ دَرْك ذَلِكَ عِلْمُ الْمَسْؤُولِ والسائل.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس: ﴿بَلِ ادَّرَكَ عِلْمُهُمْ فِي الآخِرَة﴾ أَيْ: غَابَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿بَلِ ادَّارَكَ عِلْمُهُمْ فِي الآخِرَةِ﴾ يَعْنِي: يُجَهِّلهم رَبُّهُمْ، يَقُولُ: لَمْ يَنْفُذْ لَهُمْ إِلَى الْآخِرَةِ عِلْمٌ، هَذَا قَوْلٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: "بَلْ أدْرَكَ عِلْمُهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ" حِينَ لَمْ يَنْفَعِ الْعِلْمُ، وَبِهِ قَالَ عَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: أَنَّ عِلْمَهُمْ إِنَّمَا يُدرك وَيَكْمُلُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ حَيْثُ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ ذَلِكَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَسْمِعْ بِهِمْ وَأَبْصِرْ يَوْمَ يَأْتُونَنَا لَكِنِ الظَّالِمُونَ الْيَوْمَ فِي ضَلالٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٣٨] .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَقْرَأُ: "بَلْ أَدْرَكَ عِلْمُهُمْ" قَالَ: اضْمَحَلَّ عِلْمُهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، حِينَ عَايَنُوا الْآخِرَةَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ هُمْ فِي شَكٍّ مِنْهَا﴾ عَائِدٌ عَلَى الْجِنْسِ، وَالْمُرَادُ الْكَافِرُونَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَعُرِضُوا عَلَى رَبِّكَ صَفًّا لَقَدْ جِئْتُمُونَا كَمَا خَلَقْنَاكُمْ أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ بَلْ زَعَمْتُمْ أَلَّنْ نَجْعَلَ لَكُمْ مَوْعِدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٤٨] أَيِ: الْكَافِرُونَ مِنْكُمْ. وَهَكَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿بَلْ هُمْ فِي شَكٍّ مِنْهَا﴾ أَيْ: شاكُّون فِي وُجُودِهَا وَوُقُوعِهَا، ﴿بَلْ هُمْ مِنْهَا عَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي عمَاية وَجَهْلٍ كَبِيرٍ فِي أَمْرِهَا وَشَأْنِهَا.

---

## 27:67-70 — verses 67-70 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about those among the polytheists who deny the resurrection: that they considered it far-fetched that bodies could be brought back after becoming bones, decayed remains, and dust. Then He said: {We have indeed been promised this, we and our fathers before, before} that is: we have continually heard this, we and our fathers, and we see no reality or occurrence of it.

Their statement: {This is nothing but the legends of the ancients} they mean: this promise of the return of bodies is nothing but the legends of the ancients, that is: a people took it from those before them, and those before them received it one from another, and it has no reality.

God Almighty says, responding to them concerning what they supposed of disbelief and denial of the resurrection: {Say}, O Muhammad, to these people: {Travel through the land and see how the end of the criminals was} that is, those who denied the messengers and what they brought them concerning the matter of the resurrection and other things: how God's vengeance, punishment, and exemplary chastisement befell them, while God saved from among them His noble messengers and those believers who followed them. This indicates the truthfulness and validity of what the messengers brought.

Then the Almighty says, consoling His Prophet ﷺ: {And do not grieve over them} that is, over those who denied what you brought, and do not sorrow over them nor let your soul waste away in regrets over them. {And do not be in distress over what they plot} that is, concerning their scheming against you and their rejection of what you brought, for God is your supporter and your helper, and He will make your religion manifest over whoever opposes it and stands in stubborn defiance against it, in the east and in the west.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ مُنْكِرِي الْبَعْثِ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ: أَنَّهُمُ اسْتَبْعَدُوا إِعَادَةَ الْأَجْسَادِ بَعْدَ صَيْرُورَتِهَا عِظَامًا وَرُفَاتًا وَتُرَابًا، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿لَقَدْ وُعِدْنَا هَذَا نَحْنُ وَآبَاؤُنَا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ أَيْ: مَا زِلْنَا نَسْمَعُ بِهَذَا نَحْنُ وَآبَاؤُنَا، وَلَا نَرَى لَهُ حَقِيقَةً وَلَا وُقُوعًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُمْ: ﴿إِنْ هَذَا إِلا أَسَاطِيرُ الأوَّلِينَ﴾ : يَعْنُونَ: مَا هَذَا الْوَعْدُ بِإِعَادَةِ الْأَبْدَانِ، ﴿إِلا أَسَاطِيرُ الأوَّلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَخَذَهُ قَوْمٌ عَمَّن قَبْلَهُمْ، مَنْ قَبْلِهُمْ يَتَلَقَّاهُ بَعْضٌ عَنْ بَعْضٍ، وَلَيْسَ لَهُ حَقِيقَةٌ.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مُجِيبًا لَهُمْ عَمَّا ظَنُّوهُ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَعَدَمِ الْمَعَادِ: ﴿قُلْ﴾ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -لِهَؤُلَاءِ: ﴿سِيرُوا فِي الأرْضِ فَانْظُرُوا كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الْمُجْرِمِينَ﴾ أَيِ: المكذِّبين بِالرُّسُلِ وَمَا جَاءُوهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ أَمْرِ الْمَعَادِ وَغَيْرِهِ، كَيْفَ حَلَّتْ بِهِمْ نقَمُ اللَّهِ وَعَذَابُهُ وَنَكَالُهُ، ونجَّى اللَّهُ مِنْ بَيْنِهِمْ رُسُلَهُ الْكِرَامَ وَمَنْ اتَّبَعَهُمْ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَدَلَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى صِدْقِ مَا جَاءَتْ بِهِ الرُّسُلُ وَصِحَّتِهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُسَلِّيًا لِنَبِيِّهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ: ﴿وَلا تَحْزَنْ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيِ: الْمُكَذِّبِينَ بِمَا جِئْتَ بِهِ، وَلَا تَأْسَفْ عَلَيْهِمْ وَتَذْهَبْ نَفْسُكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسَرَاتٍ، ﴿وَلا تَكُ فِي ضَيْقٍ مِمَّا يَمْكُرُونَ﴾ أي: فِي كَيْدِكَ ورَدّ مَا جِئْتَ بِهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مُؤَيِّدُكَ وَنَاصِرُكَ، ومظهرٌ دِينَكَ عَلَى مَنْ خَالَفَهُ وَعَانَدَهُ فِي الْمَشَارِقِ وَالْمَغَارِبِ.

---

## 27:71-75 — verses 71-75 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about the polytheists, concerning their questioning about the Day of Resurrection and their considering its occurrence far-fetched: {And they say, "When will this promise be, if you are truthful?"} God says in answer to them: {Say}, O Muhammad, {perhaps there has come near to you some of that which you seek to hasten}. [Ibn Abbas said: that it has drawn near, or that it will be brought near, to you, some of that which you seek to hasten]. Mujahid, al-Dahhak, Ata al-Khurasani, Qatadah, and al-Suddi said likewise.

This is what is meant by His saying, the Exalted: {And they say, "When will it be?" Say, "Perhaps it is near"} [al-Isra: 51], and the Exalted said: {They seek to hasten you with the punishment, and indeed Hell will encompass the disbelievers} [al-Ankabut: 54].

The "lam" (the preposition "for/to") entered into His saying {radifa lakum, has come near to you} because it carries within it the meaning of "has been hastened for you," as Mujahid said in a report from him: {perhaps there has come near to you}, meaning, has been hastened for you.

Then God, the Exalted, said: {And indeed your Lord is possessed of bounty upon mankind}, meaning, in His lavishing His favors upon them despite their wronging themselves, while they, in spite of that, do not give Him thanks for it, except a few of them. {And indeed your Lord surely knows what their breasts conceal and what they declare}, meaning, He knows the secrets and the inner thoughts just as He knows what is outwardly apparent. {It is the same, among you, whether one conceals his speech or proclaims it} [al-Ra'd: 10], {He knows the secret and what is even more hidden} [Ta Ha: 7], {Unquestionably, when they cover themselves with their garments, He knows what they conceal and what they declare} [Hud: 5].

Then the Exalted informs that He is the Knower of the unseen of the heavens and the earth, and that He is the Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, that is, what is absent from His servants and what they witness. He said: {And there is nothing absent in the heaven and the earth}. Ibn Abbas said: meaning, there is nothing, {in the heaven and the earth, but it is in a clear register}. This is like His saying, the Exalted: {Do you not know that God knows what is in the heaven and the earth? Indeed that is in a register; indeed that is easy for God} [al-Hajj: 70].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، فِي سُؤَالِهِمْ عَنْ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَاسْتِبْعَادِهِمْ وُقُوعَ ذَلِكَ: ﴿وَيَقُولُونَ مَتَى هَذَا الْوَعْدُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾ قَالَ اللَّهُ مُجِيبًا لَهُمْ: ﴿قُلْ﴾ يَا مُحَمَّدُ ﴿عَسَى أَنْ يَكُونَ رَدِفَ لَكُمْ بَعْضُ الَّذِي تَسْتَعْجِلُونَ﴾ . [قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ أَنْ يَكُونَ قَرُبَ -أَوْ: أَنْ يُقَرَّبَ -لَكُمْ بَعْضُ الَّذِي تَسْتَعْجِلُونَ] . وَهَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَعَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ.

وَهَذَا هُوَ الْمُرَادُ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَقُولُونَ مَتَى هُوَ قُلْ عَسَى أَنْ يَكُونَ قَرِيبًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٥١] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿يَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ بِالْعَذَابِ وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمُحِيطَةٌ بِالْكَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ: ٥٤] .

وَإِنَّمَا دَخَلَتِ "اللَّامُ" فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿رَدِفَ لَكُمْ﴾ ؛ لِأَنَّهُ ضُمن مَعْنَى "عَجِل لَكُمْ" كَمَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ: ﴿عَسَى أَنْ يَكُونَ رَدِفَ لَكُمْ﴾ : عَجِلَ لَكُمْ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَذُو فَضْلٍ عَلَى النَّاسِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي إِسْبَاغِهِ نعمَه عَلَيْهِمْ مَعَ ظُلْمِهِمْ لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَهُمْ مَعَ ذَلِكَ لَا يَشْكُرُونَهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ إِلَّا الْقَلِيلُ مِنْهُمْ، ﴿وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَيَعْلَمُ مَا تُكِنُّ صُدُورُهُمْ وَمَا يُعْلِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْلَمُ السَّرَائِرَ وَالضَّمَائِرَ، كَمَا يَعْلَمُ الظَّوَاهِرَ، ﴿سَوَاءٌ مِنْكُمْ مَنْ أَسَرَّ الْقَوْلَ وَمَنْ جَهَرَ بِهِ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ١٠] ، ﴿يَعْلَمُ السِّرَّ وَأَخْفَى﴾ [طَهَ: ٧] ، ﴿أَلا حِينَ يَسْتَغْشُونَ ثِيَابَهُمْ يَعْلَمُ مَا يُسِرُّونَ وَمَا يُعْلِنُونَ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٥] .

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى بِأَنَّهُ عَالِمُ غَيْبِ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ، وَأَنَّهُ عَالِمُ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ -وَهُوَ مَا غَابَ عَنِ الْعِبَادِ وَمَا شَاهَدُوهُ -فَقَالَ: ﴿وَمَا مِنْ غَائِبَةٍ فِي السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي: وَمَا مِنْ شَيْءٍ، ﴿فِي السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ تَعْلَمْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ إِنَّ ذَلِكَ فِي كِتَابٍ إِنَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَسِيرٌ﴾ [الحج: ٧٠] .

---

## 27:76-81 — verses 76-81 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about His mighty Book and what it contains of guidance, clear proofs, and discernment between truth and falsehood: it relates to the Children of Israel, who are the bearers of the Torah and the Gospel, {most of that concerning which they differ}, such as their disagreement and divergence concerning Jesus (peace be upon him). The Jews fabricated lies, while the Christians went to excess, so the Qur'an came to them with the moderate, true, and just statement: that he is a servant among the servants of God and one of His noble prophets and messengers, upon him be the best of blessings and peace, as the Exalted said: {That is Jesus, son of Mary, the word of truth about which they dispute} [Maryam: 34].

Regarding His statement: {And indeed it is guidance and mercy for the believers}, that is, guidance for the hearts of the believers, and a mercy for them in matters of practice.

Then He said: {Indeed your Lord will judge between them}, that is, on the Day of Resurrection, {by His judgment, and He is the Mighty}, in His vengeance, {the All-Knowing}, of the deeds and words of His servants.

{So rely upon God}, that is, in your affairs, and convey the message of your Lord, {for indeed you are upon the manifest truth}, that is, you are upon the manifest truth even if those who oppose you do oppose you, among those for whom wretchedness has been decreed and against whom the word of your Lord has been established, that they will not believe even if every sign were to come to them. For this reason He said: {Indeed you cannot make the dead hear}, that is, you cannot make them hear anything that would benefit them. Likewise, these people have a covering over their hearts, and in their ears is the heaviness of disbelief. For this reason He said: {Indeed you cannot make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear the call when they turn their backs and retreat. Nor can you guide the blind out of their error. You can only make hear those who believe in Our signs, and they are the ones who submit} [meaning]: only he who is truly hearing and seeing will respond to you, the hearing and seeing that is beneficial being that which resides in the heart and the inner insight that submits to God and to what has come from Him through the tongues of the messengers, upon them be peace.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ كِتَابِهِ الْعَزِيزِ، وَمَا اشْتَمَلَ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالْبَيِّنَاتِ وَالْفُرْقَانِ : إِنَّهُ يَقُصُّ عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ -وَهُمْ حَمَلَةُ التَّوْرَاةِ وَالْإِنْجِيلِ - ﴿أَكْثَرَ الَّذِي هُمْ فِيهِ يَخْتَلِفُونَ﴾ ، كَاخْتِلَافِهِمْ فِي عِيسَى وَتَبَايُنِهِمْ فِيهِ، فَالْيَهُودُ افْتَرَوْا، وَالنَّصَارَى غَلَوا، فَجَاءَ [إِلَيْهِمُ] الْقُرْآنُ بِالْقَوْلِ الْوَسَطِ الْحَقِّ الْعَدْلِ: أَنَّهُ عَبْدٌ مِنْ عِبَادِ اللَّهِ وَأَنْبِيَائِهِ وَرُسُلِهِ الْكِرَامِ، عَلَيْهِ [أَفْضَلُ] الصَّلَاةِ وَالسَّلَامِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ذَلِكَ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ قَوْلَ الْحَقِّ الَّذِي فِيهِ يَمْتَرُونَ﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٣٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّهُ لَهُدًى وَرَحْمَةٌ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: هُدًى لِقُلُوبِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَرَحْمَةٌ لَهُمْ فِي الْعَمَلِيَّاتِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ رَبَّكَ يَقْضِي بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿بِحُكْمِهِ وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ﴾ فِي انْتِقَامِهِ، ﴿الْعَلِيمُ﴾ بِأَفْعَالِ عِبَادِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِمْ.

﴿فَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَى اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي أُمُورِكَ، وبَلّغ رِسَالَةَ رَبِّكَ، ﴿إِنَّكَ عَلَى الْحَقِّ الْمُبِينِ﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتَ عَلَى الْحَقِّ الْمُبِينِ وَإِنْ خَالَفَكَ مَنْ خَالَفَكَ، مِمَّنْ كُتِبَتْ عَلَيْهِ الشَّقَاوَةُ وحَقَّت عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ، وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّكَ لَا تُسْمِعُ الْمَوْتَى﴾ أَيْ: لَا تُسْمِعُهُمْ شَيْئًا يَنْفَعُهُمْ، فَكَذَلِكَ هَؤُلَاءِ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ غِشَاوَةٌ، وَفِي آذَانِهِمْ وَقْر الْكُفْرِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّكَ لَا تُسْمِعُ الْمَوْتَى وَلا تُسْمِعُ الصُّمَّ الدُّعَاءَ إِذَا وَلَّوْا مُدْبِرِينَ * وَمَا أَنْتَ بِهَادِي الْعُمْيِ عَنْ ضَلالَتِهِمْ إِنْ تُسْمِعُ إِلا مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِآيَاتِنَا فَهُمْ مُسْلِمُونَ﴾ [أَيْ] : إِنَّمَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَكَ مَنْ هُوَ سَمِيعٌ بَصِيرٌ، السَّمْعُ وَالْبَصَرُ النافعُ فِي الْقَلْبِ وَالْبَصِيرَةِ الْخَاضِعُ لِلَّهِ، وَلِمَا جَاءَ عَنْهُ عَلَى أَلْسِنَةِ الرُّسُلِ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ.

---

## 27:82 — verse 82

### Translation

This beast will emerge at the end of time, when people have become corrupt, have abandoned God's commands, and have altered the true religion. God will bring forth for them a beast from the earth, it is said from Mecca, and it is said from elsewhere, as will be detailed later, and it will speak to the people concerning that.

Ibn Abbas, al-Hasan, and Qatadah said, and it is reported from Ali (may God be pleased with him): "it will speak to them" means it will address them directly.

Ata al-Khurasani said: it will speak to them, saying to them: "Indeed the people did not have certainty in Our signs." This is also related from Ali, and Ibn Jarir preferred this view. But there is an evident problem with this view, and God knows best.

Ibn Abbas said, in one report: it will wound them. And in another report from him, he said: it does both, meaning this and that. This is a good view, and there is no contradiction between them, and God knows best.

Many hadiths and reports have come down mentioning the beast, so let us mention what is readily available of them, and God is the one whose help is sought:

Imam Ahmad said: Sufyan reported to us, from Furat, from Abu al-Tufayl, from Hudhayfah ibn Asid al-Ghifari, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ looked out upon us from an upper room while we were discussing the matter of the Hour, and he said: "The Hour will not come until you see ten signs: the sun rising from its place of setting, the smoke, the beast, the emergence of Gog and Magog, the coming down of Jesus son of Mary, the Dajjal (Antichrist), and three sinkings: a sinking in the west, a sinking in the east, and a sinking in the Arabian Peninsula, and a fire that emerges from the depths of Aden which drives, or gathers, the people, spending the night with them wherever they spend the night, and resting with them at midday wherever they rest."

This is how Muslim and the compilers of the Sunan collections narrated it, through various routes, from Furat al-Qazzaz, from Abu al-Tufayl Amir ibn Wathilah, from Hudhayfah as a mawquf (halted report). Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (sound, good). Muslim also narrated it from the hadith of Abd al-Aziz ibn Rufay', from Abu al-Tufayl, from him, as a marfu' (raised report, attributed to the Prophet). And God knows best.

Another route: Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said, from Talhah ibn Amr and Jarir ibn Hazim. As for Talhah, he said: Abdullah ibn Ubaydullah ibn Umayr al-Laythi informed me, that Abu al-Tufayl reported to him, from Hudhayfah ibn Asid al-Ghifari, Abu Sarihah. As for Jarir, he said: from Abdullah ibn Ubayd, from a man from the family of Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, and the hadith of Talhah is more complete and better, he said: The Messenger of God ﷺ mentioned the beast and said: "It will have three emergences over time. It will emerge once from the far desert, and news of it will not reach the town," meaning Mecca, "then it will remain hidden for a long time, then it will emerge again, a lesser emergence than that one, and news of it will spread among the people of the desert, and news of it will reach the town," meaning Mecca. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Then, while the people are in the greatest of mosques in sanctity before God and the noblest of them, the Sacred Mosque, nothing will alarm them except that it will be bellowing between the Corner and the Station, shaking the dust off its head. The people will scatter away from it, separately and together, and a group of believers will remain, knowing that they cannot escape God. It will begin with them, brightening their faces until they become like a shining star, then it will turn away across the earth, and no seeker can catch it, nor can any fleeing one escape it, so much so that a man will seek refuge from it in prayer, and it will come to him from behind and say: 'O so-and-so, now you pray?' and he will turn to face it, and it will brand his face, then it will move on. And the people will share in wealth and accompany one another in the cities, the believer known from the disbeliever, so much so that the believer will say: 'O disbeliever, pay me my due,' and the disbeliever will say: 'O believer, pay me my due.'"

Ibn Jarir narrated it through two routes, from Hudhayfah ibn Asid, as a mawquf report, and God knows best. He also narrated it from the report of Hudhayfah ibn al-Yaman as a marfu' report, stating that this would occur in the time of Jesus son of Mary, while he is circling the Kaaba, but its chain of transmission is not sound.

Another hadith: Muslim ibn al-Hajjaj said: Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah reported to us, Muhammad ibn Bishr reported to us, from Abu Hayyan, from Abu Zur'ah, from Abdullah ibn Amr, who said: I memorized a hadith from the Messenger of God ﷺ that I have not forgotten since. I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "The first of the signs to appear will be the sun rising from its place of setting and the emergence of the beast upon the people in the forenoon. Whichever of the two occurs before the other, the other will follow closely after it."

Another hadith: Muslim narrated in his Sahih from the hadith of al-Ala ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn Ya'qub, the freedman of al-Huraqah, from his father, from Abu Hurairah, may God be pleased with him, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Hasten to do good deeds before six things: the sun rising from its place of setting, the smoke, the Dajjal, the beast, or the particular matter that concerns each one of you, or the general matter." And he also has, from the hadith of Qatadah, from al-Hasan, from Ziyad ibn Rabah, from Abu Hurairah, may God be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Hasten to do good deeds before six things: the Dajjal, the smoke, the beast of the earth, the sun rising from its place of setting, the general matter, and the particular matter that concerns each one of you."

Another hadith: Ibn Majah said: Harmalah ibn Yahya reported to us, Ibn Wahb reported to us, Amr ibn al-Harith and Ibn Lahi'ah informed me, from Yazid ibn Abi Habib, from Sinan ibn Sa'd, from Anas ibn Malik, may God be pleased with him, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, who said: "Hasten to do good deeds before six things: the sun rising from its place of setting, the smoke, the beast of the earth, the Dajjal, the particular matter that concerns each one of you, and the general matter." He alone narrated it thus.

Another hadith: Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi also said: Hammad ibn Salamah reported to us, from Ali ibn Zayd, from Aws ibn Khalid, from Abu Hurairah, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The beast of the earth will emerge, and with it will be the staff of Moses and the seal of Solomon (peace be upon them both), and it will strike the nose of the disbeliever with the staff and brighten the face of the believer with the seal, until people gather at the table and the believer is known from the disbeliever."

Imam Ahmad narrated it from Bahz, Affan, and Yazid ibn Harun, all three from Hammad ibn Salamah, with this wording, and he said: "It will strike the nose of the disbeliever with the seal and brighten the face of the believer with the staff, so much so that the people sharing one table will gather, and this one will say: 'O believer,' and that one will say: 'O disbeliever.'"

Ibn Majah narrated it from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah, from Yunus ibn Muhammad al-Mu'addib, from Hammad ibn Salamah, with this wording.

Another hadith: Ibn Majah said: Abu Ghassan Muhammad ibn Amr reported to us, Abu Tumaylah reported to us, Khalid ibn Ubayd reported to us, Abdullah ibn Buraydah reported to us, from his father, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ took me to a place in the desert near Mecca, and there was dry land surrounded by sand, and the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The beast will emerge from this spot," indicating a small span within a handspan's width.

Ibn Buraydah said: I performed the pilgrimage some years after that, and he showed us a staff of his, and it was exactly like this staff of mine, such and such.

Abd al-Razzaq said, from Ma'mar, from Qatadah: that Ibn Abbas said: It is a beast covered with fine hair, having four legs, and it will emerge from one of the valleys of Tihamah.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father reported to us, Abdullah ibn Raja' reported to us, Fudayl ibn Marzuq reported to us, from Atiyyah, who said: Abdullah said: The beast will emerge from a crack in al-Safa, running like a galloping horse for three days, and even a third of it will not yet have come out.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Aban ibn Salih, who said: Abdullah ibn Amr was asked about the beast, and he said: The beast will emerge from beneath a rock at Jiyad. By God, if I were with them, or if I wished, I could point with my staff to the rock from beneath which the beast will emerge. It was said: Then what will it do, O Abdullah ibn Amr? He said: It will face the east and let out a cry that will penetrate it, then it will face Syria and let out a cry that will penetrate it, then it will face the west and let out a cry that will penetrate it, then it will face Yemen and let out a cry that will penetrate it, then it will set out from Mecca in the evening and arrive by morning at Usfan. It was said: Then what? He said: I do not know.

From Abdullah ibn Umar, that he said: The beast will emerge on the night of Jam' (Muzdalifah). Ibn Abi Hatim narrated it, and in its chain is Ibn al-Baylamani.

From Wahb ibn Munabbih: that he related from the speech of Uzayr (peace be upon him), that he said: "And a beast will emerge from beneath Sodom, speaking to the people, each one of them hearing it, and pregnant women will give birth before their term, and sweet water will turn bitter, and close friends will become enemies, and wisdom will be burned away, and knowledge will be lifted up, and the land adjoining it will speak. And in that time people will hope for what they cannot attain, and toil for what they cannot reach, and work for what they will not eat." Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this from him.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father reported to us, Abu Salih the scribe of al-Layth reported to us, Mu'awiyah ibn Salih reported to me, from Abu Maryam: that he heard Abu Hurairah, may God be pleased with him, say: The beast has something of every color in it, and the distance between its two horns is a parasang for a rider.

Ibn Abbas said: it is like a huge spear.

From the Commander of the Faithful, Ali ibn Abi Talib, may God be pleased with him, that he said: It is a beast having feathers, fine hair, and a hoof, and it has no tail, but it has a beard, and it can outrun a swift galloping horse for three days, and even a third of it will not yet have emerged. Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Ibn al-Zubayr, that he described the beast, saying: its head is the head of a bull, its eye is the eye of a pig, its ear is the ear of an elephant, its horn is the horn of a stag, its neck is the neck of an ostrich, its chest is the chest of a lion, its color is the color of a leopard, its flank is the flank of a cat, its tail is the tail of a ram, and its legs are the legs of a camel, with twelve cubits between each two joints. With it will emerge the staff of Moses and the seal of Solomon. No believer will remain except that it marks a white mark on his face with the staff of Moses, and that mark spreads until his whole face turns white because of it. And no disbeliever will remain except that it marks a black mark on his face with the seal of Solomon, and that mark spreads until his whole face turns black because of it, so much so that people in the markets will say when trading: "How much for this, O believer? How much for this, O disbeliever?" And so much so that the members of a household, sitting at their table, will know their believer from their disbeliever among them. Then the beast will say to them: "O so-and-so, rejoice, you are among the people of Paradise," and "O so-and-so, you are among the people of the Fire." That is the meaning of God's saying, Exalted is He: {And when the word befalls them, We will bring forth for them a beast from the earth speaking to them, that the people did not have certainty in Our signs.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ الدَّابَّةُ تَخْرُجُ فِي آخِرِ الزَّمَانِ عِنْدَ فَسَادِ النَّاسِ وتَرْكِهم أَوَامِرَ اللَّهِ وَتَبْدِيلِهِمُ الدِّينَ الْحَقَّ، يُخْرِجُ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ دَابَّةً مِنَ الْأَرْضِ -قِيلَ: مِنْ مَكَّةَ. وَقِيلَ: مِنْ غَيْرِهَا. كَمَا سَيَأْتِي تَفْصِيلُهُ -فَتُكَلِّم النَّاسَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وقَتَادَةُ -ورُوي عَنْ عَلِيٍّ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ -: تُكَلِّمُهُمْ كَلَامًا أَيْ: تُخَاطِبُهُمْ مُخَاطَبَةً.

وَقَالَ عَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ: تُكَلِّمُهُمْ فَتَقُولُ لَهُمْ: إِنَّ النَّاسَ كَانُوا بِآيَاتِنَا لَا يُوقِنُونَ. وَيُرْوَى هَذَا عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ. وَفِي هَذَا [الْقَوْلِ] نَظَرٌ لَا يَخْفَى، وَاللَّهُ أعلم.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ -فِي رِوَايَةٍ -تَجْرَحُهُمْ. وَعَنْهُ رِوَايَةٌ، قَالَ: كُلًّا تَفْعَلُ يَعْنِي هَذَا وَهَذَا، وَهُوَ قولٌ حَسَنٌ، وَلَا مُنَافَاةَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي ذِكْرِ الدَّابَّةِ أَحَادِيثُ وَآثَارٌ كَثِيرَةٌ، فَلْنَذْكُرْ مَا تَيَسَّرَ مِنْهَا، وَاللَّهُ الْمُسْتَعَانُ:

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ فُرَات، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ، عَنْ حُذَيفة بْنِ أَسِيدٍ الْغِفَارِيِّ قَالَ: أَشْرَفَ عَلَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنْ غُرْفَةٍ وَنَحْنُ نَتَذَاكَرُ أَمْرَ السَّاعَةَ فَقَالَ: لَا تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ حَتَّى تَرَوا عَشْرَ آيَاتٍ: طُلُوعُ الشَّمْسِ مِنْ مَغْرِبِهَا، وَالدُّخَانُ، والدابة، وخروج يأجوج ومأجوج، وخروج عيسى بن مَرْيَمَ، وَالدَّجَّالُ، وَثَلَاثَةُ خُسُوفٍ: خَسْفٌ بِالْمَغْرِبِ، وَخَسْفٌ بِالْمَشْرِقِ، وَخَسْفٌ بِجَزِيرَةِ الْعَرَبِ، وَنَارٌ تَخْرُجُ مِنْ قَعر عَدَنٍ تَسُوقُ -أَوْ: تَحْشُرُ -النَّاسَ، تَبِيتُ مَعَهُمْ حَيْثُ بَاتُوا، وَتَقِيلُ مَعَهُمْ حَيْثُ قَالُوا" .

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ فُرَات الْقَزَّازِ، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ عَامِرِ بْنِ وَاثِلَةَ، عَنْ حُذَيفة مَوْقُوفًا . وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ . وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ أَيْضًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ رُفَيْع، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ، عَنْهُ مَرْفُوعًا . وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

طَرِيقٌ أُخْرَى: قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ، عَنْ طَلْحَةَ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، وَجَرِيرِ بْنِ حَازِمٍ، فَأَمَّا طَلْحَةُ فَقَالَ: أَخْبَرَنِي عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عمَير اللِّيثِيُّ: أَنَّ أَبَا الطُّفَيْلِ حَدَّثَهُ، عَنْ حذَيفة بْنِ أَسِيدٍ الْغِفَارِيِّ أَبِي سَريحَةَ، وَأَمَّا جَرِيرٌ فَقَالَ: عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُبيد، عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ آلِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ -وَحَدِيثُ طَلْحَةَ أَتَمُّ وَأَحْسَنُ -قَالَ: ذَكَرَ رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ الدَّابَّةَ فَقَالَ: "لَهَا ثَلَاثُ خَرْجَاتٍ مِنَ الدَّهْرِ، فَتَخْرُجُ خَرجة مِنْ أَقْصَى الْبَادِيَةِ، وَلَا يَدْخُلُ ذِكْرُهَا الْقَرْيَةَ -يَعْنِي: مَكَّةَ -ثُمَّ تَكْمُنُ زَمَانًا طَوِيلًا ثُمَّ تَخْرُجُ خَرْجة أُخْرَى دُونَ تِلْكَ، فَيَعْلُو ذِكْرُهَا فِي أَهْلِ الْبَادِيَةِ، وَيَدْخُلُ ذِكْرُهَا الْقَرْيَةَ" يَعْنِي: مَكَّةَ. -قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "ثُمَّ بَيْنَمَا النَّاسُ فِي أَعْظَمِ الْمَسَاجِدِ عَلَى اللَّهِ حُرْمَةً وَأَكْرَمِهَا: الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ، لَمْ يَرُعْهم إِلَّا وَهِيَ تَرْغو بَيْنَ الرُّكْنِ وَالْمَقَامِ، تَنْفُضُ عَنْ رَأْسِهَا التُّرَابَ. فَارْفَضَّ النَّاسُ عَنْهَا شتَّى وَمَعًا، وَبَقِيَتْ عِصَابَةٌ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَعَرَفُوا أَنَّهُمْ لَمْ يُعْجِزُوا اللَّهَ، فَبَدَأَتْ بِهِمْ فجَلَت وُجُوهَهُمْ حَتَّى جَعَلَتْهَا كَأَنَّهَا الْكَوْكَبُ الدُّرِّيُّ، وَوَلَّتْ فِي الْأَرْضِ لَا يُدْرِكُهَا طَالِبٌ، وَلَا يَنْجُو مِنْهَا هَارِبٌ، حَتَّى إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لِيَتَعَوَّذُ مِنْهَا بِالصَّلَاةِ، فَتَأْتِيهِ مِنْ خَلْفِهِ فَتَقُولُ: يَا فُلَانُ، الآن تصلي؟ فَيُقْبِلُ عَلَيْهَا فَتَسِمُهُ فِي وَجْهِهِ، ثُمَّ تَنْطَلِقُ وَيَشْتَرِكُ النَّاسُ فِي الْأَمْوَالِ، وَيَصْطَحِبُونَ فِي الْأَمْصَارِ، يُعْرَفُ الْمُؤْمِنُ مِنَ الْكَافِرِ، حَتَّى إِنَّ الْمُؤْمِنَ لَيَقُولُ: يَا كَافِرُ، اقْضِنِي حَقِّي. وَحَتَّى إِنَّ الْكَافِرَ لَيَقُولُ: يَا مُؤْمِنُ، اقْضِنِي حَقِّي" .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ مِنْ طَرِيقَيْنِ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ أُسَيْد مَوْقُوفًا فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَرَوَاهُ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ الْيَمَانِ مَرْفُوعًا، وَأَنَّ ذَلِكَ فِي زمان عيسى بن مَرْيَمَ، وَهُوَ يَطُوفُ بِالْبَيْتِ، وَلَكِنَّ إِسْنَادَهُ لَا يَصِحُّ .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ مُسْلِمُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي حَيَّان، عَنْ أَبِي زُرْعَة، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: حَفظْتُ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَدِيثًا لَمْ أَنْسَهُ بَعْدُ: سمعتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنْ أَوَّلَ الْآيَاتِ خُرُوجًا طُلُوعُ الشَّمْسِ مِنْ مَغْرِبِهَا، وَخُرُوجُ الدَّابَّةِ عَلَى النَّاسِ ضُحى، وَأَيَّتُهُمَا مَا كَانَتْ قَبْلَ صَاحِبَتِهَا، فَالْأُخْرَى عَلَى إِثْرِهَا قَرِيبًا" .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: رَوَى مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْعَلَاءِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ يَعْقُوبَ -مَوْلَى الحُرَقَة -عَنْ أَبِيهِ: عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "بَادِرُوا بِالْأَعْمَالِ سِتًّا : طُلُوعَ الشَّمْسِ مِنْ مَغْرِبِهَا، أَوِ الدُّخَانَ، أَوِ الدَّجَّالَ، أَوِ الدَّابَّةَ، أَوْ خَاصَّةَ أَحَدِكُمْ، أَوْ أَمْرَ الْعَامَّةِ" . وَلَهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ رَبَاحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "بَادِرُوا بِالْأَعْمَالِ سِتًّا: الدَّجَّالَ، وَالدُّخَانَ، وَدَابَّةَ الْأَرْضِ، وَطُلُوعَ الشَّمْسِ مِنْ مَغْرِبِهَا، وَأَمْرَ الْعَامَّةِ وخُويّصة أَحَدِكُمْ" .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ ابْنُ مَاجَةَ: حَدَّثَنَا حَرْمَلَة بْنُ يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ وابن لَهِيعة، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، عَنْ سِنَان بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "بَادِرُوا بِالْأَعْمَالِ سِتًا: طُلُوعَ الشَّمْسِ مِنْ مَغْرِبِهَا، وَالدُّخَانَ، وَدَابَّةَ الْأَرْضِ، وَالدَّجَّالَ، وخُوَيّصة أَحَدِكُمْ، وَأَمْرَ الْعَامَّةِ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَوْسِ بْنِ خَالِدٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "تَخْرُجُ دَابَّةُ الْأَرْضِ، وَمَعَهَا عَصَا مُوسَى وَخَاتَمُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، فَتَخْطِمُ أَنْفَ الْكَافِرِ بِالْعَصَا، وتُجلي وجه المؤمن بِالْخَاتَمِ، حَتَّى يَجْتَمِعَ النَّاسُ عَلَى الْخُوَانِ يُعْرَفُ الْمُؤْمِنُ مِنَ الْكَافِرِ".

وَرَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ بَهْز وَعَفَّانَ وَيَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، ثَلَاثَتُهُمْ عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، بِهِ . وَقَالَ: "فَتَخْطِمُ أَنْفَ الْكَافِرِ بِالْخَاتَمِ، وَتَجْلُو وَجْهَ الْمُؤْمِنِ بِالْعَصَا، حَتَّى إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْخُوَانِ الْوَاحِدِ لَيَجْتَمِعُونَ فَيَقُولُ هَذَا: يَا مُؤْمِنُ، وَيَقُولُ هَذَا: يَا كَافِرُ".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أبي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ الْمُؤَدَّبِ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، بِهِ .

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو غَسَّانَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو تُمَيْلة، حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدُ بْنُ عُبَيْد، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ بُرَيدة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: ذَهَبَ بِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَى مَوْضِعٍ بِالْبَادِيَةِ، قَرِيبٍ مِنْ مَكَّةَ، فَإِذَا أَرْضٌ يَابِسَةٌ حَوْلَهَا رَمْلٌ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "تَخْرُجُ الدَّابَّةُ مِنْ هَذَا الْمَوْضِعِ. فَإِذَا فِتْر فِي شِبْرٍ".

قَالَ ابْنُ بُرَيدة: فَحَجَجْتُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ بِسِنِينَ، فَأَرَانَا عَصًا لَهُ، فَإِذَا هُوَ بعَصاي هَذِهِ ، كَذَا وَكَذَا .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ؛ أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: هِيَ دابةٌ ذَاتُ زَغَب، لَهَا أَرْبَعُ قَوَائِمَ، تَخْرُجُ مِنْ بَعْضِ أَوْدِيَةِ تِهَامَةَ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ رَجَاء، حَدَّثَنَا فُضَيْلُ بْنُ مَرْزُوقٍ، عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: تَخْرُجُ الدَّابَّةُ مِنْ صِدْع مِنَ الصَّفَا كجَرْي الْفَرَسِ ثَلَاثَةَ أَيَّامٍ، لَمْ يَخْرُجْ ثُلُثُهَا.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبَانَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ قَالَ: سُئِلَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو عَنِ الدَّابَّةِ، فَقَالَ: الدَّابَّةُ تَخْرُجُ مِنْ تَحْتِ صَخْرَةٍ بِجِيَادٍ، وَاللَّهِ لَوْ كُنْتُ مَعَهُمْ -أَوْ لَوْ شِئْتُ بِعَصَايَ الصَّخْرَةَ الَّتِي تَخْرُجُ الدَّابَّةُ مِنْ تَحْتِهَا. قِيلَ: فتصنعُ مَاذَا يَا عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو؟ قَالَ: تَسْتَقْبِلُ الْمَشْرِقَ فَتَصْرُخُ صَرْخَةً تنفُذُه، ثُمَّ تَسْتَقْبِلُ الشَّامَ فَتَصْرُخُ صَرْخَةً تُنْفِذُهُ، ثُمَّ تَسْتَقْبِلُ الْمَغْرِبَ فَتَصْرُخُ صَرْخَةً تُنْفِذُهُ، ثُمَّ تَسْتَقْبِلُ الْيَمَنَ فَتَصْرُخُ صَرْخَةً تُنْفِذُهُ، ثُمَّ تَرُوحُ مِنْ مَكَّةَ فَتُصْبِحُ بِعُسْفَانَ. قِيلَ: ثُمَّ مَاذَا؟ قَالَ: لَا أَعْلَمُ.

وَعَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: تَخْرُجُ الدَّابَّةُ لَيْلَةَ جَمْع . وَرَوَاهُ ابن أبي حاتم. وفي إِسْنَادِهِ ابْنُ الْبَيْلَمَانِ .

وَعَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ مُنَبِّهٍ: أَنَّهُ حَكَى مِنْ كَلَامٍ عُزَير، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: وَتَخْرُجُ مِنْ تَحْتِ سَدُومَ دَابَّةٌ تُكَلِّمُ النَّاسَ كُلٌّ يَسْمَعُهَا، وَتَضَعُ الْحَبَالَى قَبْلَ التَّمَامِ، وَيَعُودُ الْمَاءُ الْعَذْبُ أُجَاجًا، وَيَتَعَادَى الْأَخِلَّاءُ، وتُحرَقُ الْحِكْمَةُ، ويُرفَعُ الْعِلْمُ، وَتُكَلِّمُ الْأَرْضُ الَّتِي تَلِيهَا. وَفِي ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ يَرْجُو النَّاسُ مَا لَا يَبْلُغُونَ، وَيَتْعَبُونَ فِيمَا لَا يَنَالُونَ، وَيَعْمَلُونَ فِيمَا لَا يَأْكُلُونَ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو صَالِحٍ -كَاتَبِ اللَّيْثِ -حَدَّثَنِي مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَقُولُ: إِنَّ الدَّابَّةَ فِيهَا مِنْ كُلِّ لَوْنٍ، مَا بَيْنَ قَرْنَيْهَا فَرْسَخٌ لِلرَّاكِبِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هِيَ مِثْلُ الْحَرْبَةِ الضَّخْمَةِ.

وَعَنْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: إِنَّهَا دَابَّةٌ لَهَا رِيشٌ وَزَغَبٌ وَحَافِرٌ، وَمَا لَهَا ذَنَبٌ، وَلَهَا لِحْيَةٌ، وَإِنَّهَا لَتُخْرِجُ حُضْر الْفَرَسِ الْجَوَادِ ثَلَاثًا، وَمَا خَرَجَ ثُلُثُهَا . وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنِ ابْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ أَنَّهُ وَصَفَ الدَّابَّةَ فَقَالَ: رَأْسُهَا رَأْسُ ثَوْرِ، وَعَيْنُهَا عَيْنُ خِنْزِيرٍ، وَأُذُنُهَا أُذُنُ فِيلٍ، وَقَرْنُهَا قَرْنُ أيَّل، وَعُنُقُهَا عُنُقُ نَعَامَةٍ، وَصَدْرُهَا صَدْرُ أَسَدٍ، وَلَوْنُهَا لَوْنُ نَمر، وَخَاصِرَتُهَا خَاصِرَةُ هِرّ، وَذَنَبُهَا ذَنَبُ كَبْشٍ، وَقَوَائِمُهَا قَوَائِمُ بَعِيرٍ، بَيْنَ كُلِّ مَفْصَلَيْنِ اثْنَا [عَشَرَ] ذِرَاعًا، تَخْرُجُ مَعَهَا عَصَا مُوسَى، وَخَاتَمُ سُلَيْمَانَ، فَلَا يَبْقَى مُؤْمِنٌ إِلَّا نَكتَت فِي وَجْهِهِ بِعَصَا مُوسَى نُكْتَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فَتَفْشُو تِلْكَ النُّكْتَةُ حَتَّى يَبْيَضَّ لَهَا وَجْهُهُ، وَلَا يَبْقَى كَافِرٌ إِلَّا نَكَتت فِي وَجْهِهِ نُكْتَةً سَوْدَاءَ بِخَاتَمِ سُلَيْمَانَ، فَتَفْشُو تِلْكَ النُّكْتَةُ حَتَّى يَسْوَدَّ لَهَا وَجْهُهُ، حَتَّى إِنَّ النَّاسَ يَتَبَايَعُونَ فِي الْأَسْوَاقِ: بِكَمْ ذَا يَا مُؤْمِنُ، بِكَمْ ذَا يَا كَافِرُ؟ وَحَتَّى إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْبَيْتِ يَجْلِسُونَ عَلَى مَائِدَتِهِمْ، فَيَعْرِفُونَ مُؤْمِنَهُمْ مِنْ كَافِرِهِمْ، ثُمَّ تَقُولُ لَهُمُ الدَّابَّةُ: يَا فُلَانُ، أَبْشِرْ، أَنْتَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ، وَيَا فُلَانُ، أَنْتَ مِنْ أَهْلِ النَّارِ. فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا وَقَعَ الْقَوْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَخْرَجْنَا لَهُمْ دَابَّةً مِنَ الأرْضِ تُكَلِّمُهُمْ أَنَّ النَّاسَ كَانُوا بِآيَاتِنَا لَا يُوقِنُونَ﴾ .

---

## 27:83-86 — verses 83-86 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the Day of Resurrection and the gathering of the wrongdoers who denied the signs of Allah and His messengers, brought before Allah, Mighty and Majestic, so that He may question them about what they did in the worldly abode, as a rebuke, a reproach, a belittling and a humiliation. He says: {And [warn of] the Day when We will gather from every nation a troop}, meaning: from every people and generation a troop, that is, a group, {of those who deny Our signs}, just as the Almighty said: {Gather those who did wrong, and their kinds} [al-Saffat: 22], and the Almighty said: {And when the souls are paired} [al-Takwir: 7].

As for His saying {and they are driven in ranks}, Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them, said: they are pushed forward. Qatadah said: drivers (wazaʿah) hold back the first of them until the last of them catches up. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: they are driven along.

{Until, when they come}, meaning: when they are made to stand before Allah, Mighty and Majestic, in the place of questioning, {He will say, "Did you deny My signs while you had no comprehensive knowledge of them, or what was it you were doing?"}, meaning: they are asked about their beliefs and their deeds. Since they were not among the people of felicity, and were as Allah the Almighty said of them: {And he did not affirm truth, nor did he pray. But he denied and turned away} [al-Qiyamah: 31-32], the proof was thus established against them, and they had no excuse to offer, just as the Almighty said: {This is a Day on which they will not speak, nor will they be permitted to offer excuses. Woe, that Day, to the deniers} [al-Mursalat: 35-37]. And likewise He says here: {And the word will befall them for the wrong they did, and they will not speak}, meaning: they will be struck dumb and will have no answer, because in the worldly abode they had been wrongdoers against themselves, and now they have been returned to the Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, from whom nothing hidden is concealed.

Then the Almighty says, drawing attention to His complete power, His mighty dominion, and His exalted station which requires obedience to Him, submission to His commands, and belief in His prophets regarding the truth they brought, from which there is no swerving: {Do they not see that We made the night that they might rest in it?}, meaning: in it is darkness by reason of which their movements grow still, their breaths grow calm, and they rest from the fatigue of exertion during their day. {And the day giving sight}, meaning: illuminating and radiant. By reason of that they go about their livelihoods, their earnings, their travels and their trade, and other matters of theirs which they need. {Indeed, in that are signs for a people who believe}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَحَشْرِ الظَّالِمِينَ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ إِلَى بَيْنَ يَدَيِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، لِيَسْأَلَهُمْ عَمَّا فَعَلُوهُ فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا، تَقْرِيعًا وَتَوْبِيخًا، وَتَصْغِيرًا وَتَحْقِيرًا فَقَالَ: ﴿وَيَوْمَ نَحْشُرُ مِنْ كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ فَوْجًا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ كُلِّ قَوْمٍ وَقَرْنٍ فَوْجًا، أَيْ: جَمَاعَةً، ﴿مِمَّنْ يُكَذِّبُ بِآيَاتِنَا﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿احْشُرُوا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا وَأَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ٢٢] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿وَإِذَا النُّفُوسُ زُوِّجَتْ﴾ [التَّكْوِيرِ: ٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَهُمْ يُوزَعُونَ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: يُدْفَعُونَ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَزَعَةٌ تَرُدُّ أَوَّلَهُمْ عَلَى آخِرِهِمْ. وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: يُسَاقُونَ.

﴿حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءُوا﴾ أَيْ: أُوقِفُوا بَيْنَ يَدَيِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فِي مَقَامِ الْمُسَاءَلَةِ، ﴿قَالَ أَكَذَّبْتُمْ بِآيَاتِي وَلَمْ تُحِيطُوا بِهَا عِلْمًا أَمْ مَاذَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَيُسْأَلُونَ عَنِ اعْتِقَادِهِمْ، وَأَعْمَالِهِمْ فَلَمَّا لَمْ يَكُونُوا مِنْ أَهْلِ السَّعَادَةِ، وَكَانُوا كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى عَنْهُمْ: ﴿فَلا صَدَّقَ وَلا صَلَّى. وَلَكِنْ كَذَّبَ وَتَوَلَّى﴾ [الْقِيَامَةِ: ٣١، ٣٢] ، فَحِينَئِذٍ قَامَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الْحُجَّةُ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ عُذْرٌ يَعْتَذِرُونَ بِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَذَا يَوْمُ لَا يَنْطِقُونَ وَلا يُؤْذَنُ لَهُمْ فَيَعْتَذِرُونَ. وَيْلٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِلْمُكَذِّبِينَ﴾ [الْمُرْسَلَاتِ: ٣٥، ٣٧] ، وَهَكَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَوَقَعَ الْقَوْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِمَا ظَلَمُوا فَهُمْ لَا يَنْطِقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بُهِتُوا فَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ جَوَابٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا ظَلَمَةً لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَقَدْ رُدُّوا إِلَى عَالِمِ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ الَّذِي لَا تَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ خَافِيَةٌ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُنَبِّهًا عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ التَّامَّةِ، وَسُلْطَانِهِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَشَأْنِهِ الرَّفِيعِ الَّذِي تَجِبُ طَاعَتُهُ وَالِانْقِيَادُ لِأَوَامِرِهِ، وَتَصْدِيقِ أَنْبِيَائِهِ فِيمَا جَاءُوا بِهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ الَّذِي لَا مَحيد عَنْهُ، فَقَالَ ﴿أَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّا جَعَلْنَا اللَّيْلَ لِيَسْكُنُوا فِيهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِيهِ ظَلَامٌ تَسْكُنُ بِسَبَبِهِ حَرَكَاتُهُمْ، وَتَهْدَأُ أَنْفَاسُهُمْ، وَيَسْتَرِيحُونَ مِنْ نَصَب التَّعَبِ فِي نَهَارِهِمْ. ﴿وَالنَّهَارَ مُبْصِرًا﴾ أَيْ: مُنِيرًا مُشْرِقًا، فَبِسَبَبِ ذَلِكَ يَتَصَرَّفُونَ فِي الْمَعَايِشِ والمكاسب، والأسفار والتجارات، وغير ذلك من شؤونهم الَّتِي يَحْتَاجُونَ إِلَيْهَا، ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ .

---

## 27:87-90 — verses 87-90 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted is He, tells of the terror of the day of the blast of fright in the Trumpet, which, as it comes in the hadith, is "a horn that is blown into." And in the hadith of (the Trumpet) it is said that Israfil is the one who blows into it by the command of God, exalted is He. He blows into it first the blast of fright and prolongs it, and that is at the end of the life of this world, when the Hour comes upon the worst of people among the living, so that whoever is in the heavens and whoever is on the earth is terrified, {except whom God wills}, and they are the martyrs, for they are alive with their Lord, given provision.

The Imam Muslim ibn al-Hajjaj said: [chain] ... Abdullah ibn Amr, may God be pleased with him, and a man came to him and said: "What is this talk you have been relating, that the Hour will come at such and such a time?" He said: "Glory be to God" or "There is no god but God" or a word similar to these, "I had resolved never to tell anyone anything again. I only said: you will soon see, after a little while, a tremendous matter that will destroy the House, and such and such will happen." Then he said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The Dajjal will emerge among my nation and will remain forty, I do not know whether he said forty days, or forty months, or forty years, then God will send Jesus son of Mary, as though he were Urwah ibn Mas'ud, and he will seek him out and destroy him. Then people will remain for seven years with no enmity between any two of them. Then God will send a cold wind from the direction of Syria, and no one will remain on the face of the earth in whose heart is even the weight of a mote of good or faith except that it will take him, so that even if one of them entered into the depths of a mountain, it would enter upon him there until it took him." He said: I heard this from the Messenger of God ﷺ. He said: "Then there will remain the worst of people, as light as birds and as senseless as the minds of predatory beasts, recognizing no good and disapproving of no evil. Satan will appear to them in a form and say: 'Will you not respond?' They will say: 'What do you command us?' So he will command them to worship idols, and they will be, in that state, with abundant provision and a good life. Then the Trumpet will be blown, and no one will hear it except that he will tilt one side of his neck and raise the other." He said: "The first to hear it will be a man patching the trough of his camels." He said: "So he will fall dead, and the people will fall dead. Then God will send, or he said, will send down rain like dew, or he said, like shade, (al-Nu'man, the narrator, was uncertain), and from it the bodies of people will sprout. Then it will be blown into a second time, and at once they will be standing, looking about. Then it will be said: 'O people, come to your Lord,' and they will be made to stand, for they are to be questioned. Then it will be said: 'Bring forth the levy of the Fire.' It will be said: 'From how many?' It will be said: 'From every thousand, nine hundred and ninety-nine.'" He said: "That is a day that will turn children grey-haired, and that is the day when the leg will be uncovered."

As for his saying, "Then the Trumpet will be blown, and no one will hear it except that he will tilt one side of his neck and raise the other," the "layt" is the side surface of the neck, meaning he tilts his neck in order to listen well to what comes from the sky.

This is the blast of fright. Then after that comes the blast of swooning, which is death. Then after that comes the blast of rising to stand before the Lord of the worlds, which is the resurrection from the graves for all created beings. Hence He said: {And all come to Him in humble submission} (this can be read with a long vowel, or without it, as a verb; both readings carry the same meaning), and {dakhirin} means submissive, obedient, no one lagging behind His command, just as He, exalted is He, said: {The day He will call you and you will respond with His praise} [al-Isra: 52], and He said: {Then when He calls you with a single call from the earth, at once you will come forth} [al-Rum: 25]. And in the hadith of the Trumpet it is said that at the third blast, God commands the souls, and they are placed in a hole in the Trumpet. Then Israfil blows into it after the bodies have sprouted in their graves and their places. When the Trumpet is blown, the souls fly forth, the souls of the believers glowing with light, and the souls of the disbelievers with darkness. Then God, mighty and majestic, will say: "By My might and My majesty, every soul shall surely return to its body." So the souls come to their bodies and creep into them as poison creeps into one who has been stung. Then they rise up and shake the dust from their graves, as God, exalted is He, said: {The day they will come forth from the graves swiftly, as if they were racing toward a target} [al-Ma'arij: 43].

His saying, {And you see the mountains, thinking them firmly fixed, while they pass by like clouds passing}, means: you see them as though they were still fixed, remaining as they were, while they pass by like the passing of clouds, that is, they depart from their places, just as He, exalted is He, said: {The day the sky will shake with a violent shaking, and the mountains will move with a moving} [al-Tur: 9, 10], and He said: {And they ask you about the mountains, so say: My Lord will scatter them completely, and leave the earth a level, flat plain, wherein you see no crookedness and no unevenness} [Taha: 105, 107], and He, exalted is He, said: {And the day We shall set the mountains in motion, and you will see the earth exposed} [al-Kahf: 47].

His saying, {The doing of God, who has perfected all things}, means: He does that by His tremendous power, He who has perfected everything He has created and has instilled in it whatever wisdom He has instilled. {Indeed He is well aware of what you do}, meaning: He knows what His servants do of good and evil, and He will requite them accordingly.

Then He, exalted is He, clarifies the state of the fortunate and the wretched on that day, saying: {Whoever comes with a good deed will have better than it}, Qatadah said: this refers to sincerity (ikhlas). Zayn al-Abidin said: it is the statement "there is no god but God." It has been made clear elsewhere that he will have ten times its like. {And they will be safe that day from terror}, just as He said in another verse: {The greatest terror will not grieve them} [al-Anbiya: 103], and He said: {Is he who is cast into the Fire better, or he who comes secure on the Day of Resurrection} [Fussilat: 40], and He said: {And they will be secure in the high chambers} [Saba: 37].

His saying, {And whoever comes with an evil deed, their faces will be thrust into the Fire}, means: whoever meets God having done evil, with no good deed to his credit, or whose evil deeds outweigh his good deeds, each according to his case. Hence He said: {Are you rewarded except for what you used to do?}

Ibn Mas'ud, Abu Hurayrah, Ibn Abbas (may God be pleased with them), Anas ibn Malik, Ata, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ikrimah, Mujahid, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, Abu Wa'il, Abu Salih, Muhammad ibn Ka'b, Zayd ibn Aslam, al-Zuhri, al-Suddi, al-Dahhak, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and Ibn Zayd all said, regarding His saying, {And whoever comes with an evil deed}, that it means: with polytheism (shirk).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ هَوْلِ يَوْمِ نَفْخَةِ الفَزَع فِي الصُّور، وَهُوَ كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "قَرْنٌ يُنْفَخُ فِيهِ". وَفِي حَدِيثِ (الصُّور) أَنَّ إِسْرَافِيلَ هُوَ الَّذِي يَنْفُخُ فِيهِ بِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، فَيَنْفُخُ فِيهِ أَوَّلًا نَفْخَةَ الْفَزَعِ وَيُطَوِّلُهَا، وَذَلِكَ فِي آخِرِ عُمْرِ الدُّنْيَا، حِينَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ عَلَى شَرَارِ النَّاسِ مِنَ الْأَحْيَاءِ، فَيَفْزَعُ مَنْ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ ومَنْ فِي الْأَرْضِ ﴿إِلا مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ﴾ ، وَهُمُ الشُّهَدَاءُ، فَإِنَّهُمْ أَحْيَاءٌ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ يُرْزَقُونَ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ مُسْلِمُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ: حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنِ مُعاذ الْعَنْبَرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ سَالِمٍ: سَمِعْتُ يَعْقُوبَ بْنَ عَاصِمِ بْنِ عُرْوَة بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ الثَّقَفِيَّ، سَمِعْتُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَجَاءَهُ رَجُلٌ فَقَالَ: مَا هَذَا الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي تَحدث إِنَّ السَّاعَةَ تَقُومُ إِلَى كَذَا وَكَذَا؟ فَقَالَ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ -أَوْ: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ -أَوْ كَلِمَةً نَحْوَهُمَا -لَقَدْ هَمَمْتُ أَلَّا أُحَدِّثَ أَحَدًا شَيْئًا أَبَدًا، إِنَّمَا قُلْتُ: إِنَّكُمْ سَتَرَوْنَ بَعْدَ قَلِيلٍ أَمْرًا عَظِيمًا يُخَرِّبُ الْبَيْتُ، وَيَكُونُ وَيَكُونُ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَخْرُجُ الدَّجَّالُ فِي أُمَّتِي فَيَمْكُثُ أَرْبَعِينَ -[لَا أَدْرِي أَرْبَعِينَ] يَوْمًا، أَوْ أَرْبَعِينَ شَهْرًا، أَوْ أَرْبَعِينَ عَامًا -فَيَبْعَثُ الله عيسى بن مَرْيَمَ كَأَنَّهُ عُرْوَةُ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، فَيَطْلُبُهُ فَيُهْلِكُهُ. ثُمَّ يَمْكُثُ النَّاسُ سَبْعَ سِنِينَ، لَيْسَ بَيْنَ اثْنَيْنِ عَدَاوَةٌ، ثُمَّ يُرْسِلُ اللَّهُ رِيحًا بَارِدَةً مِنْ قِبَلِ الشَّامِ، فَلَا يَبْقَى عَلَى وَجْهِ الْأَرْضِ أَحَدٌ فِي قَلْبِهِ مِثْقَالُ ذَرَّةٍ مِنْ خَيْرٍ أَوْ إِيمَانٍ إِلَّا قَبَضَتْهُ، حَتَّى لَوْ أَنَّ أَحَدَهُمْ دَخَلَ فِي كَبَدِ جَبَلٍ لدخَلَتْه عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى تَقْبِضَهُ". قَالَ: سَمِعْتُهَا مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، قَالَ: "فَيَبْقَى شِرَارُ النَّاسِ فِي خِفَّةِ الطَّيْرِ وَأَحْلَامِ السِّبَاعِ، لَا يَعْرِفُونَ مَعْرُوفًا وَلَا يُنْكِرُونَ مُنْكَرًا، فَيَتَمَثَّلُ لَهُمُ الشَّيْطَانُ فَيَقُولُ: أَلَا تَسْتَجِيبُونَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: فَمَا تَأْمُرُنَا؟ فَيَأْمُرُهُمْ بِعِبَادَةِ الْأَوْثَانِ، وَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ دَارٌّ رِزْقُهُمْ، حسنٌ عَيْشُهُمْ. ثُمَّ يُنْفَخُ فِي الصُّورِ فَلَا يَسْمَعُهُ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا أَصْغَى لِيتًا [وَرَفَعَ لِيتًا] . قَالَ: "وَأَوَّلُ مَنْ يَسْمَعُهُ رَجُلٌ يَلُوط حَوْضَ إِبِلِهِ". قَالَ: "فَيَصْعَقُ ويَصعقُ النَّاسُ، ثُمَّ يُرْسِلُ اللَّهُ -أَوْ قَالَ: يُنْزِلُ اللَّهُ مَطَرًا كَأَنَّهُ الطَّل -أَوْ قَالَ: الظِّلُّ -نُعْمَانُ الشَّاكُّ -فَتَنْبُتُ مِنْهُ أَجْسَادُ النَّاسِ، ثُمَّ ينفَخُ فِيهِ أُخْرَى فَإِذَا هُمْ قِيَامٌ يَنْظُرُونَ. ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، هَلُمُّوا إِلَى رَبِّكُمْ، وَقِفُوهُمْ إِنَّهُمْ مسؤولون. ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: أَخْرِجُوا بَعْثَ النَّارِ. فَيُقَالُ: مِنْ كَمْ؟ فَيُقَالُ: مِنْ كُلِّ أَلْفٍ تِسْعَمِائَةٍ وَتِسْعَةً وَتِسْعِينَ". قَالَ: "فَذَلِكَ يَوْمٌ يَجْعَلُ الْوِلْدَانَ شَيْبًا، وَذَلِكَ يَوْمَ يُكْشَفُ عَنْ سَاقٍ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ : ثُمَّ يُنْفَخُ فِي الصُّورِ فَلَا يَسْمَعُهُ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا أَصْغَى لِيتًا وَرَفَعَ لِيتًا" اللِّيتُ : هُوَ صَفْحَةُ الْعُنُقِ، أَيْ: أَمَالَ عُنُقَهُ لِيَسْتَمِعَهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ جَيِّدًا.

فَهَذِهِ نَفْخَةُ الْفَزَعِ. ثُمَّ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ نَفْخَةُ الصَّعْقِ، وَهُوَ الْمَوْتُ. ثُمَّ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ نَفْخَةُ الْقِيَامِ لِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ، وَهُوَ النُّشُورُ مِنَ الْقُبُورِ لِجَمِيعِ الْخَلَائِقِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَكُلٌّ أَتَوْهُ دَاخِرِينَ﴾ -قُرئ بِالْمَدِّ، وَبِغَيْرِهِ عَلَى الْفِعْلِ، وكلٌ بِمَعْنًى وَاحِدٍ -وَ ﴿دَاخِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: صَاغِرِينَ مُطِيعِينَ، لا يتخلف أحد عَنْ أَمْرِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يَدْعُوكُمْ فَتَسْتَجِيبُونَ بِحَمْدِهِ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٥٢] ، وَقَالَ ﴿ثُمَّ إِذَا دَعَاكُمْ دَعْوَةً مِنَ الأرْضِ إِذَا أَنْتُمْ تَخْرُجُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٢٥] . وَفِي حَدِيثِ الصُّورِ: أَنَّهُ فِي النَّفْخَةِ الثَّالِثَةِ يَأْمُرُ اللَّهُ الْأَرْوَاحَ، فَتُوضَعُ فِي ثُقْبٍ فِي الصُّورِ، ثُمَّ يَنْفُخُ إِسْرَافِيلُ فِيهِ بَعْدَمَا تَنْبُتُ الْأَجْسَادُ فِي قُبُورِهَا وَأَمَاكِنِهَا، فَإِذَا نُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ طَارَتِ الْأَرْوَاحُ، تَتَوَهَّجُ أَرْوَاحُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ نُورًا، وَأَرْوَاحُ الْكَافِرِينَ ظُلمة، فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: وَعِزَّتِي وَجَلَالِي لَتَرْجِعَنَّ كُلُّ رُوحٍ إِلَى جَسَدِهَا. فَتَجِيءُ الْأَرْوَاحُ إِلَى أَجْسَادِهَا، فَتَدِبُّ فِيهَا كَمَا يَدب السُّمُّ فِي اللَّدِيغِ، ثُمَّ يَقُومُونَ فَيَنْفُضُونَ التُّرَابَ مِنْ قُبُورِهِمْ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يَخْرُجُونَ مِنَ الأجْدَاثِ سِرَاعًا كَأَنَّهُمْ إِلَى نُصُبٍ يُوفِضُونَ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ٤٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَرَى الْجِبَالَ تَحْسَبُهَا جَامِدَةً وَهِيَ تَمُرُّ مَرَّ السَّحَابِ﴾ أَيْ: تَرَاهَا كَأَنَّهَا ثَابِتَةٌ بَاقِيَةٌ عَلَى مَا كَانَتْ عَلَيْهِ، وَهِيَ تَمُرُّ مَرَّ السَّحَابِ، أَيْ: تَزُولُ عَنْ أَمَاكِنِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تَمُورُ السَّمَاءُ مَوْرًا وَتَسِيرُ الْجِبَالُ سَيْرًا﴾ [الطُّورِ: ٩، ١٠] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَيَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْجِبَالِ فَقُلْ يَنْسِفُهَا رَبِّي نَسْفًا فَيَذَرُهَا قَاعًا صَفْصَفًا لَا تَرَى فِيهَا عِوَجًا وَلا أَمْتًا﴾ [طَهَ: ١٠٥، ١٠٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَوْمَ نُسَيِّرُ الْجِبَالَ وَتَرَى الأرْضَ بَارِزَةً﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٤٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿صُنْعَ اللَّهِ الَّذِي أَتْقَنَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْعَلُ ذَلِكَ بِقُدْرَتِهِ الْعَظِيمَةِ الَّذِي قَدْ أَتْقَنَ كُلَّ مَا خَلَقَ، وَأَوْدَعَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْحِكْمَةِ مَا أَوْدَعَ، ﴿إِنَّهُ خَبِيرٌ بِمَا تَفْعَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ عَلِيمٌ بِمَا يَفْعَلُ عِبَادُهُ مِنْ خَيْرٍ وَشَرٍّ فَيُجَازِيهِمْ عَلَيْهِ.
